- 2026-05-14 Phase 9 - Key in-sample structural finding worth flagging for Checkpoint B/C/D: BTC K=3 shows P(low->high)=0.004 and P(high->low)=0.000. If this 'transitions only via mid-vol' structure persists on the holdout, it is a substantive crypto-vol-dynamics finding. If it shatters, the regime model is unstable and the experiment fails by design. Either outcome is real evidence.

- 2026-05-14 Checkpoint A - Mahmoud reviews checkpoint_B_validation_plan.md (M1 no-regime baseline, M2 BTC K=4 model applied to ETH/SOL via forward algorithm only, M3 generalization measure, M4 aggregate >=2 of 3 rule). - 2026-05-14 Checkpoint A - Honest pre-flight warning recorded for Checkpoint B: cross-coin transfer of HMMs trained on RAW (un-standardized) features is a stringent test. ETH/SOL feature scales differ from BTC. Aggregate STOP at Checkpoint B is a real possible outcome and would be archived as a negative finding, not 'rescued' by post-hoc feature standardization.

- 2026-05-14 Checkpoint B - Mahmoud reads checkpoint_B_decision_packet.md and signs ONE of A/B/C: (A) PROCEED per mechanical rule (recommended; unblocks bootstrap-CI step then Checkpoint C); (B) STOP-and-archive (conservative override of mechanical PROCEED); (C) RE-SCOPE with fresh preregistration. - 2026-05-14 Checkpoint B - Key finding for the trading bot record: BTC's K=4 regime structure transfers to ETH (positive cross-coin generalization, +990 LL improvement over no-regime baseline) but NOT to SOL (negative absolute LL under BTC's model). On RAW daily log-return + 20-day rolling-vol features. The asymmetry is feature-scale-driven; the experiment did not 'rescue' it via standardization. This is in-sample evidence only; the holdout pass at Checkpoint D will reveal whether the BTC<->ETH coherence is persistent or in-sample-specific.

- 2026-05-14 Checkpoint B signed - Mahmoud authorizes the bootstrap-CI run when ready: 'Authorize bootstrap-CI step per the plan.' The mechanism: DD>45% bear-rule trigger fires on volatility-driven drawdowns inside bull years, and the priority order routes bear before bull is checked. Three honest paths forward, each requires SEPARATE explicit authorization: (1) **PHASE 4L v2 RE-DESIGN with direction-conditional bear rule** - simplest fix. Change bear_contraction rule from "annual<-20% OR DD>45% OR bear_conf>25%" to "annual<-0% AND (DD>45% OR bear_conf>25%)". This requires the bear DD trigger to co-occur with a non-positive annual return. Predicted re-classification: 2020/2021 -> NOT bear (their annual returns are positive); 2022 still bear (annual=-65%). Cost: low; one tool edit + threshold-stability re-test on the same 5 windows. (2) **PHASE 4L v2 RE-DESIGN with new mode "volatile_bull_expansion"** - taxonomy expansion. Add a 5th mode for high-return + high-DD + high-vol + bull-share-dominant windows. Predicted assignments: 2020 -> volatile_bull_expansion; 2021 -> volatile_bull_expansion or chop_uncertainty; 2022/2023/2024 unchanged. Higher cost (new mode + new playbook label + tests) but more honestly captures the actual market character. (3) **PHASE 4L v2 RE-DESIGN with learned thresholds via leave-one-window-out cross-validation** - principled but expensive. Requires building a tiny optimization tool + selecting an objective function (likely "agreement with manual labels"). High cost, low marginal benefit over (1) at this sample size (5 windows is too few for stable CV). RECOMMENDED OPERATOR DECISION: do (1) first as cheapest principled fix. If (1) re-classifies 2020/2021 to bull_recovery and 2022/2023/2024 stay where they are, ship the v2 and move on. If (1) leaves 2020 stuck in bear because the +301% return is masked by the 54% DD breaking bull_recovery's DD<35% ceiling, then escalate to (2) and add volatile_bull_expansion. DO NOT proceed to coupling-reduced features (Phase 4J v2 ETHUSDT/SOLUSDT path) until threshold stability is restored on BTCUSDT alone. NO live data, NO broker, NO promotion at any path. The combination of K9 ≥ 100 trades over the ~6.6y combined IS+OOS window with DR10 annual_turnover < 0.50 is structurally incompatible with K9-clearing active-trading at retail-scale start_cash on liquid futures (contract-quantization issue) and on cash equities at standard 0.5% risk sizing.

## 2026-05-27 - Framework-level DR10 SEAL revision INVESTIGATION plan authored (PLAN ONLY; 7 governance options; no recommendation; no SEAL revision performed)

- **Plan file:** `docs/framework_dr10_revision_investigation_plan_after_s13_d1_terminal.md` (507 lines; sha `450373a3c4fbc039058b1ff410dc4e92c95093e86028e254c580624458a04546`)
- **Authorization:** `Authorize framework-level DR10 SEAL revision investigation PLAN only.` (Path T6 from the post-s13-d1 next-track selection plan)
- **Document type:** investigation PLAN; **NOT a SEAL revision**; **NOT a candidate spec**; **NOT a threshold proposal as binding**. Scopes out what a future SEAL revision turn would need; does not perform the revision.
- **Investigation question (formalized in §2):** is the current DR10 `annual_turnover > 0.50` threshold mathematically incompatible with K9 ≥ 100 for active-trading strategies on liquid futures / cash equities at practical retail-scale start_cash ($100k–$1M)?
- **Sub-Q1 answer (mathematically derived in §4-§5):** NO compatibility at retail scale on liquid futures (contract-quantization). Cash equities clear joint K9 + DR10 only at unrealistic nano-sizing (0.005–0.02% risk per trade).
- **Key derived constraint (§4.1, §4.5):** `per_trade_notional ≤ 0.5% × start_cash` to satisfy both K9 (OOS ≥ 50 trades/y) AND DR10 (`annual_turnover ≤ 0.50`).
- **At $200k start_cash → max per-trade notional ≤ $1,000.** Liquid futures contract minimum notional ranges $20k (M2K) to $130k (6E) — all infeasible. Cash equity 2-5 shares of $200-500 stocks is feasible but trivial.
- **Capital-scale binding analysis (§5.2):** active futures trading clears K9 ∧ DR10 only at start_cash ≥ ~$10M (institutional scale). Cash-equity active trading at standard 0.5% risk clears at start_cash ≥ ~$5M.
- **Historical candidate audit (§6):** every actively-traded s9/s10/s11/s12/s13-lineage candidate that progressed to IS execution had observed or estimated annual_turnover >> 0.50. **s13-d1 was the first to reach P6.5 with K9 cleared and edge positive, exposing the latent DR10 turnover-branch constraint.** Prior candidates terminated at upstream gates (K9 inviolate, DR9 data integrity) before DR10 could fire.
- **7 governance options enumerated (§7; presented with math trade-offs, framework consequences, migration cost, defensibility; NO option recommended):**
    - **A — Status quo:** DR10 unchanged. Framework targets buy-and-hold-with-rebalance OR institutional-scale active trading. Affirms intent. Migration cost zero.
    - **B — Raise threshold:** scalar revision (e.g., 5.0, 15.0, 25.0, 100.0). At 100.0 s13-d1's 84.79 would clear (turnover branch effectively disabled). Migration cost moderate.
    - **C — Drop turnover branch:** keep `S2_cost_drag > 0.05` only. Original DR10 name was "turnover_COST_explosion" — implies cost was the load-bearing concern. s13-d1 cost_drag 2.35% would NOT have fired. Migration cost low.
    - **D — Asset-class-specific:** futures threshold X, equities threshold Y, ETFs threshold Z. Reflects contract-quantization reality. Migration cost high (parameter proliferation).
    - **E — Capital-scale normalize:** `threshold = 0.50 × ($1M / start_cash)`. At $200k → effective 2.50; s13-d1's 84.79 still fires. Direction-of-normalization concern noted (institutional traders are LESS sensitive to turnover-cost; counter-intuitive to be stricter at higher capital).
    - **F — OR → AND:** `annual_turnover > 0.50 AND S2_cost_drag > 0.05` (both must fire). Single-operator change. s13-d1 would NOT have fired. Removes raw-turnover screening alone.
    - **G — Defer:** no change for now; revisit later.
- **Critical clarification (preserved across all options, §7.8):** Per existing SEAL `no_dr_redefinition_post_seal=True` and `fail_safety_outcomes_terminal_for_this_candidate_record_id=True`, **s13-d1's REJECT_FAST verdict and terminal lifecycle status are byte-equivalent and binding under the OLD DR10 regardless of which option is selected.** A future SEAL revision (if any) applies ONLY to NEW SEAL turns going forward (s14+). Past sealed candidates retain old DR10 verdicts byte-equivalent.
- **SEAL revision scoping (§8; NOT performed this turn):** the SEAL revision turn (if any future authorization) would produce a fresh framework-level sealed artifact at `reports/framework_dr10_revision_seal_v2.{json,md}` with audit trail, OLD vs NEW DR10 verdict tables for all prior candidates (informational; no verdict changes), and migration rules. Sign-off requirements documented.
- **Hard boundaries held (§10; 22 attestations):** PLAN only · no SEAL · no SEAL revision · no Tier-N spec · no DRAFT · no BUILD · no code · no backtest · no fetch · no Databento · no network · no live · no candidate promotion · **no reinterpretation of DR10 in any existing sealed candidate** · **no modification of any sealed candidate artifact** · **no s13-d1/s12-d1/parked-candidate revival** · **no threshold proposal as binding** · **no specific governance option recommended** · **no `lessons.md` modification or staging** · no `review_queue.json` mutation · no production `idea_memory` mutation · no profitability claim.
- **All s13-d1 sealed artifacts verified byte-stable** (SEAL `262491c`, P1 `005cb8a`, P2 `beecd87`, P3 `24625c6`, P4 `c44fb13`, P6 `3fa479a`, P6.5 `15c4fb1`, P7 `cc1817b`; git diff against HEAD empty for those files).
- **Status (UNCHANGED):** Trading `PAUSED` · Live `BLOCKED_AT_6_GATES` · FRC `NEVER_GRANTED` · `no_strategy_optimization_authorized = True` · `no_dr_redefinition_post_seal = True` (per existing sealed candidates) · REC1-equivalent binding True · DIAGNOSTIC_ONLY_NOT_LIVE_GRADE · s13-d1 + s12-d1 lifecycles terminal · K9-reachability + DR10-reachability disciplines both binding for future PLAN authoring.
- **Awaiting operator selection of Option A / B / C / D / E / F / G, or alternative-investigation-rev2, or defer-without-pursuing.** No forward research motion until a separate authorization.
- **Next-authorization options (each separate; none initiated this turn; one per option from §7, plus alternative-investigation-rev2 and defer):**
    - **Option A:** `Authorize framework-level confirmation that DR10 remains at 0.50 (status quo; no SEAL revision).`
    - **Option B:** `Authorize framework-level DR10 SEAL revision to raise threshold to <specific value> only.` (operator specifies value)
    - **Option C:** `Authorize framework-level DR10 SEAL revision to drop turnover branch (keep S2_cost_drag only) only.`

- **What v2 does NOT address:** K9 inviolate >= 100 (unchanged) · K9-reachability discipline (unchanged) · DR10-reachability discipline (unchanged; now evaluated against v2 AND-conjunction) · other DRs (DR1-DR9 unchanged) · K-gates (unchanged) · C1-C8 safety contracts (unchanged) · any prior sealed candidate verdict (all preserved byte-equivalent under v1).
- **What v2 preserves:** both thresholds verbatim · DR10's precedence position 4 of 9 · REJECT_FAST rejection class · DA14=A byte-equivalent resolution · DA4 capital-scaling mitigation of the cost_drag branch · all SEAL invariants in existing candidates (no_dr_redefinition_post_seal=True for each).
